<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;5.02&#8195; Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Item 5.02(c) </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On February&#160;10, 2025, the Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) of Southwest Airlines Co. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) unanimously elected Tom Doxey to succeed Tammy Romo as Executive Vice President&#160;&amp; Chief Financial Officer and assume the responsibilities of the Company&#8217;s principal financial officer, effective March&#160;10, 2025, at which time Ms.&#160;Romo will step down from that role. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mr.&#160;Doxey, 45, is an experienced aviation executive, where he most recently served as President of Breeze Airways from 2022 to 2024. He also served as Senior Vice President, Technical Operations at United Airlines, Inc. (&#8220;United Airlines&#8221;) from 2019 to 2022 and CFO, Operations at United Airlines from 2016 to 2019. Mr.&#160;Doxey&#8217;s aviation career began in financial planning and fleet management roles at Allegiant Air and US Airways. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On February&#160;4, 2025, the Compensation Committee of the Board (the &#8220;Committee&#8221;) approved an annual base salary of $575,000 and an annual target cash short-term incentive compensation opportunity of $776,250 prorated for 2025. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Committee also approved the following structure of Mr.&#160;Doxey&#8217;s equity-based and incentive awards for the 2025 year, which are expected to be granted to him in March 2025 following his start date with the Company: </p> <p style="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:9%">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:4%;vertical-align:top;text-align:left">a)</td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left">Restricted Stock Units (&#8220;RSUs&#8221;) with a grant date fair value of $1,293,750. The RSUs will be settleable in shares of common stock and will be scheduled to vest with respect to <span style="white-space:nowrap">one-third</span> of the shares covered thereby annually, beginning March&#160;21, 2026. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:9%">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:4%;vertical-align:top;text-align:left">b)</td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left">Performance-Based Restricted Stock Units (&#8220;PBRSUs&#8221;) with a grant date fair value of $1,293,750 and a performance period of January&#160;1, 2025, through December&#160;31, 2027. The PBRSUs will have a three-year cliff vesting on February&#160;21, 2028, and will be settleable in shares of common stock. The number of PBRSUs that will vest and the number of shares of stock to be issued, if any, will be determined based on the achievement of Adjusted ROIC <span style="white-space:nowrap">(after-tax)</span> targets (as defined in the notice of grant). </p></td></tr></table>
</div></div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%;clear:both"/>

<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">

<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:9%">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:4%;vertical-align:top;text-align:left">c)</td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left">A cash award of $500,000, subject to 100% repayment if Mr.&#160;Doxey resigns or is terminated with cause within twelve months of March&#160;10, 2025, and subject to 50% repayment if Mr.&#160;Doxey resigns or is terminated with cause within 24 months of March&#160;10, 2025. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">

<td style="width:9%">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:4%;vertical-align:top;text-align:left">d)</td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left">RSUs with a grant date fair value of $1,500,000. The RSUs will be settleable in shares of common stock and will be scheduled to vest with respect to <span style="white-space:nowrap">one-third</span> of the shares covered thereby annually, beginning March&#160;21, 2026. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mr.&#160;Doxey will also enter into the Company&#8217;s form Amended and Restated Executive Service Recognition Plan Executive Employment Agreement (the &#8220;standard <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span style="white-space:nowrap">change-in-control</span></span> agreement&#8221;). The standard <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span style="white-space:nowrap">change-in-control</span></span> agreement is described in detail in the Company&#8217;s proxy statement filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission on April&#160;5, 2024, has been included as Exhibit 10.1 to the Company&#8217;s Annual Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-K</span> for the year ended December&#160;31, 2024, and is incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mr.&#160;Doxey does not have any relationships or transactions requiring disclosure under Item 401(d) or Item 404 of Regulation <span style="white-space:nowrap">S-K,</span> nor is he a party to any arrangement or understanding with any other person pursuant to which he was selected as an officer of the Company. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;7.01.&#8195;Regulation FD Disclosure. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On February&#160;10, 2025, the Company issued a press release announcing Mr.&#160;Doxey&#8217;s appointment as Executive Vice President&#160;&amp; Chief Financial Officer, effective March&#160;10, 2025. The press release is furnished herewith as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated by reference into this Item 7.01. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information furnished in this Item 7.01, including Exhibit 99.1, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section, nor shall such information be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, regardless of any general incorporation language in such filing, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing. </p>

<DESCRIPTION>EX-99.1
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE" STYLE="line-height:Normal">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g906464snap3.jpg" ALT="LOGO" STYLE="width:8.37292in;height:1.16667in;">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>SOUTHWEST AIRLINES ANNOUNCES TOM DOXEY AS EXECUTIVE VICE PRESIDENT&nbsp;&amp; CHIEF FINANCIAL OFFICER
</U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>DALLAS</B>&#151;Feb. 10, 2025&#151;<B><U>Southwest Airlines Co.</U></B> (NYSE: LUV) today announced that <U>Tom Doxey</U> has been named
Executive Vice President&nbsp;&amp; Chief Financial Officer effective March&nbsp;10, bringing extensive experience in aviation finance, operations, and strategic transformation.</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Tom&#146;s expertise in financial planning, fleet management, and operational leadership makes him a tremendous asset to our Executive Team as we drive
progress on our transformational plan,&#148; said <U>Bob Jordan</U>, President, Chief Executive Officer, &amp; Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors at Southwest Airlines. &#147;We are confident that his experience in strategic transformation will
be an asset as he builds upon our financial strength, operational excellence, and our deep commitment to our Employees, the investment community, and our Shareholders.&#148;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Doxey most recently served as President of Breeze Airways, where he led the airline through a successful transformation from a startup to profitability in
under two years. Under his leadership, Breeze developed a strong guest-focused brand, launched a loyalty program and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-branded</FONT> credit card, optimized its fleet and network, and became the largest NCAA
basketball charter operator in the country.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Prior to Breeze, Doxey held several leadership roles at United Airlines, including Senior Vice President of
Technical Operations and CFO of Operations. At United, he oversaw global maintenance, supply chain, and engineering teams, managing a $5&nbsp;billion budget and leading strategic initiatives, including a complex aircraft storage program during the
global pandemic. He also led United&#146;s fleet transactions and planning teams and had financial oversight for United&#146;s $18&nbsp;billion operations budget.</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Doxey&#146;s aviation career began in financial planning and fleet management roles at Allegiant Air and US Airways, where he gained deep expertise in
aircraft transactions, cost optimization, and corporate finance.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Doxey holds a Master of Business Administration from Arizona State University and a
Bachelor of Arts in Public Relations from Brigham Young University. He serves on the Advisory Board for BYU&#146;s Marriott School of Business and is a board member of the Aviation Maintenance Council. A former collegiate baseball player, he was
recognized as an Academic <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">All-Conference</FONT> athlete.</P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="right">


<IMG SRC="g906464snap2.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>ABOUT SOUTHWEST AIRLINES CO. </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Southwest Airlines Co.</U>&nbsp;operates one of the world&#146;s most admired and awarded airlines, offering its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-of-a-kind</FONT></FONT></FONT> value and Hospitality at 117 airports across 11 countries. Southwest took flight in 1971 to democratize the sky through friendly, reliable, and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-cost</FONT> air travel and now carries more air travelers flying nonstop within&nbsp;the United States&nbsp;than any other&nbsp;airline<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>. By empowering its more
than&nbsp;72,000<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;People to deliver unparalleled Hospitality, the maverick airline cherishes a passionate loyalty among more than 140&nbsp;million Customers carried in 2024. Southwest
leverages a unique legacy and mission to serve communities around the world including harnessing the power of its People and Purpose to put communities at the Heart of its success. Learn more by visiting&nbsp;<U>Southwest.com/citizenship</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
